id="h.bzf6i36qsctj" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.bzf6i36qsctj_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.bzf6i36qsctj" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.bzf6i36qsctj_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Overview</span></div></h2><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Unicode CLDR provides key building blocks for software supporting the world&#39;s languages. CLDR data is used by all </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://cldr.unicode.org/index#TOC-Who-uses-CLDR-" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">major software systems</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> (including all mobile phones) for their software internationalization and localization, adapting software to the conventions of different languages. </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic; font-variant: normal;">It is import</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic;">ant to review the </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="cldr-43#h.7s25aqdv767e" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-style: italic; text-decoration: underline;">Migration</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic;"> section for changes that might require action by implementations using CLDR directly or indirectly (eg, via ICU).</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="">CLDR 43.1 is </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="">a </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">dot release</span><span class="C9DxTc " style=""> focused on fixing specific issues. For more details for see </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="cldr-43#h.qobmda543waj" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-style: italic; text-decoration: underline;">Version 43.1 Changes</span><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">.</span></a></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">CLDR </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="">43 is</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> a </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">limited</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">-</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">submission </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">release</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="">, focusing on just a few areas</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">:</span></p><ol class="n8H08c BKnRcf " style="list-style-type: decimal; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Formatting Person Names</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Completing the data for formatting people‘s names, bringing it out of “tech preview”. For more information on the benefits of this feature, see </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://sites.google.com/unicode.org/cldr/index/downloads/cldr-42#h.xtb1v8tpviuc" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1155cc; text-decoration: underline;">Background</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="">.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Locales</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Adding substantially to the LikelySubtags data</span></p><ol class="n8H08c BKnRcf " style="list-style-type: decimal; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">This is used to find the likely writing system and country for a given language, used in normalizing locale identifiers and inheritance.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">The data has been contributed by </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="http://sil.org" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">SIL</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="">.</span></p></li></ol></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Inheritance</span></p><ol class="n8H08c BKnRcf " style="list-style-type: decimal; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Adding components to parentLocales.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Documenting the different inheritance for rgScope data, which inherits primarily by region.</span></p></li></ol></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Other data updates</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">In English, Türkiye is now the primary country name for the country code TR, and Turkey is available as an alternate. Other locales have been reviewed to see whether similar changes would be appropriate.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Name for the new timezone </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic; font-variant: normal;">Ciudad Juárez</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Structure</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Adding some structure and data needed for ICU4X and JavaScript, for calendar eras and parentLocales.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">All files have been moved from &#39;seed&#39; to &#39;common&#39;.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d lsiHE " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Collation &amp; Searching</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Treating various quote marks as equivalent at a Primary strength, also including Geresh and Gershayim.</span></p></li></ul></li></ol><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="">For details, see below.</span></p><div id="h.4excv1tcdlj2" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">increases each release</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="">. </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Faroese (fo) increased from Basic to Moderate, while </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Cherokee (chr), Lower Sorbian (dsb), and Upper font-family: &#39;Source Code Pro&#39;, Arial; font-size: 9.0pt; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline;">variant--&gt;</span></p><div id="h.q3dbkcq33h6w" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.q3dbkcq33h6w_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.q3dbkcq33h6w_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.q3dbkcq33h6w" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.q3dbkcq33h6w_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Data Changes</span></div></h2><div id="h.zgl4a1xqryo8" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h3 id="h.zgl4a1xqryo8_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q OmQG5e CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.zgl4a1xqryo8_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.zgl4a1xqryo8" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.zgl4a1xqryo8_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/cldr/charts/43/supplemental/dtd_deltas.html" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">DTD Changes</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> </span></div></h3><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-personNames.html#Contents" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline;">Person Names</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;"> (formerly in tech preview in CLDR 42)</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Changed the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">order, length, usage, formality</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> attribute values to be single elements, not sets.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Expanded the sample names, and changed two field values (</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">prefix, suffix</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">) to be more descriptive (</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">title, generation, credentials</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">), splitting the suffix because the placement may vary.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Date Eras</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Eras were accessed only by number. There are now</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> alphanumeric identifiers added with new attributes: an identifying </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">code</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> plus </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">aliases</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Calendars may inherit eras with the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">inheritEras</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> element. For example, the Japanese calendar inherits from Gregorian previous to a certain point in history.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Locales</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">parentLocale</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> elements now have an optional </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">component</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> attribute, with a value of </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">segmentations</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> or </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">collations</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">. These should be used for inheritance for those respective elements. For example, zh_Hant does not normally inherit from zh (since people would get a ransom-note effect with mixed scripts). However, collations can be designed to handle sets of characters for multiple writing systems.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Likely Subtags now have an attribute to indicate the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">origin</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, currently: </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">sil1, wikidata, special</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Cleanup</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The @MATCH values were not being tested for some entries, so the valid entries were extended for the elements: </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">cr, rbnfrule</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><div id="h.5amnyunrogt" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h3 id="h.5amnyunrogt_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q OmQG5e CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.5amnyunrogt_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.5amnyunrogt" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.5amnyunrogt_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/cldr/charts/43/delta/bcp47.html" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">BCP47</span><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;"> Data Changes</span></a></div></h3><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">A new timezone short id was added (</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">tz-mxcjs</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, for Ciudad Juárez), and the description for Istanbul updated the country spelling to Türkiye.</span></p></li></ul><div id="h.g7utm6n5n6qh" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h3 id="h.g7utm6n5n6qh_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q OmQG5e CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.g7utm6n5n6qh_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.g7utm6n5n6qh" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.g7utm6n5n6qh_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/cldr/charts/43/delta/supplemental-data.html" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">Supplemental Data Changes</span></a></div></h3><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Units</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">A new unit was added for the Beaufort scale. Translations are only provided for a few locales that are known to use it.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Unit preferences were added for floor area, rainfall speed, and snowfall speed. See </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://cldr-smoke.unicode.org/staging-dev/charts/43/delta/supplemental-data.html#Units" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Units</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> for differences.</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> </span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Locales</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Special parentLocales are added for collations and segmentations. </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> See </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://cldr-smoke.unicode.org/staging-dev/charts/43/delta/supplemental-data.html#Locale" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">Locale &gt; Parent…</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> for the differences.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Many new likely subtag mappings were added, thanks to contributions from SIL. See </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://cldr-smoke.unicode.org/staging-dev/charts/43/delta/supplemental-data.html#Likely" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Likely &gt; Subtag</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> for differences.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Transforms</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Aliases for certain Ethiopic transliterators were added.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">New </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">test</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> transliterators for Jpan, Khmr, Laoo, and Sinh scripts were added. These are intended for testing, not for production (especially for Jpan scripts, which requires NLP for acceptable results).</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> See </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/cldr/charts/43/delta/supplemental-data.html#Transform" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">Transforms</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> for the differences.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Language Info</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Preferred hours were changed for CW (Curaçao).</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Metazones</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Data was changed for 3 zones, and added new metazone for Ciudad Juárez. See </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://cldr-smoke.unicode.org/staging-dev/charts/43/delta/supplemental-data.html#Metazone" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Metazone</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><div id="h.vkfyufr10adb" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h3 id="h.vkfyufr10adb_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q OmQG5e CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.vkfyufr10adb_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.vkfyufr10adb" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.vkfyufr10adb_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Locale Changes</span></div></h3><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Person Name Data</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Expanded data was collected for sample names. These are not meant for use in production, but rather to give translators a feeling for how these names would appear with the different the name formatting patterns.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Data was also collected for more locales, and additional warning messages were added to alert translators about possible problems.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Inheritance Changes:</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> Data was added due to inheritance changes in order to maintain correctness of the data. Clients shouldn&#39;t need to take any action, but may notice a larger size. However, clients that use mechanisms such as string pools may see no growth at all.</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">CLDR data uses two kinds of inheritance: </span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">vertical </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">—</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> items inherited from parent languages (eg, fr_CA inherits from fr)</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">horizontal </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">—</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> items inherited within the same language (narrow Month translations inherit from short ones when the same value is expected for both)</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">These can affect two kinds of data:</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">missing values</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> — where the locale has no data (eg, no narrow Month translations)</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">marked values</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> — where CLDR has a special internal marker, which doesn&#39;t appear in the production data for a release. These specially marked values have always been removed from production data.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">There are a few cases where these modes of inheritance can conflict. To prevent that from happening (both in processing CLDR files and in clients), the internal data has been “</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-style: italic; font-weight: 700;">hardened</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">” — </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">marked values have been replaced by </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">explicit data values. This makes it more likely that clients that don&#39;t handle horizontal inheritance correctly will end up with the right answer.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Updates: </span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">The term </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic; font-variant: normal;">Türkiye</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="">is now used for the country instead of</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic; font-variant: normal;">Turkey</span><span class="C9DxTc " style=""> for English (the alternate spelling is also available). Where appropriate, a corresponding term is used in other languages.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Name for the new timezone </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-style: italic; font-variant: normal;">Ciudad Juárez</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">Locales</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> —The following locales were added, but only have Core level for this release.</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">North Levantine Arabic (apc), Choctaw (cho), Lombard (lmo), Papiamento (pap), Riffian (rif)</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Collation &amp; Searching</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The default collation and searching now treats various quote marks as equivalent at a Primary strength, also including Geresh and Gershayim. In</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> searching</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> they are treated as identical when ignoring case and accents; in collation they are ignored unless there are no primary differences (such as a vs b) and no preceding secondary differences (like a vs â).</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">Exemplars</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">The exemplar characters for Chinese (zh) now include all TGH 2013 Level 1 characters</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Rule-Based Number Format</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">There were various fixes to some locales: see the tickets for more information.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><div id="h.aijfnga3ogbs" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h3 id="h.aijfnga3ogbs_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q OmQG5e CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.aijfnga3ogbs_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.aijfnga3ogbs" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.aijfnga3ogbs_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="">File Changes</span></div></h3><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">New files:</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">/common/annotationsDerived/</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">bgn.xml, lij.xml, nso.xml, quc.xml, tn.xml</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">/common/main/</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">apc.xm, apc_SY.xml, cho.xml, cho_US.xml, lmo.xml, lmo_IT.xml, pap.xml, pap_AW.xml, pap_CW.xml, rif.xml, rif_MA.xml</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">/common/testData/personNameTest/</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">122 files</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">/common/testData/transforms/</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">am-Ethi-t-am-ethi-m0-geminate.txt, und-Latn-t-und-ethi-m0-aethiopi-geminate.txt, und-Latn-t-und-ethi-m0-alaloc-geminate.txt, und-Latn-t-und-ethi-m0-beta-metsehaf-geminate.txt, und-Latn-t-und-ethi-m0-ies-jes-1964-geminate.txt</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">/common/transforms/</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Japn-Latn.xml, Khmer-Latin.xml, Lao-Latin.xml, Sinhala-Latin.xml, am-Ethi-t-am-ethi-m0-geminate.xml, und-Ethi-t-und-latn-m0-aethiopi-geminate.xml, und-Ethi-t-und-latn-m0-alaloc-geminate.xml, und-Ethi-t-und-latn-m0-beta_metsehaf-geminate.xml, und-Ethi-t-und-latn-m0-ies-jes-1964-geminate.xml</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-style: italic; font-weight: 700;">Note: All files were moved from seed to common (see the Migration section)</span></p><div id="h.u9ejfxt03xgx" class="GV3q8e yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h3 id="h.u9ejfxt03xgx_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q OmQG5e CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.u9ejfxt03xgx_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.u9ejfxt03xgx" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.u9ejfxt03xgx_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">JSON Data Changes</span></div></h3><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">JSON </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">packaging changes due to the seed/main merge (</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16425" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16425</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">)</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="list-style-type: none; margin-left: 15.0pt;"><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">-modern</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> tier now reflects locales which are actually at modern, not those locales which are targeted to modern. (See </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16465" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16465</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> for a proposal to consider dropping the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">-modern</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> tier.)</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">-full</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> tier now includes all locales, including those formerly in seed. Use the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">coverageLevels.json</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> file in the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">cldr-core</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> package to filter out locales. (See the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Migration</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> section, below.) </span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">There is an &quot;</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">effectiveCoverageLevels</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">&quot; key in coverageLevels.json which contains coverage levels for sublocales.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">parentLocales.json now has new keys for collations and segmentations parent information </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">(</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16425" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16425</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">)</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">coverageLevels.json</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> has a new key, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">effectiveCoverageLevels</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, with calculated coverage levels for sublocales </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">(</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16425" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16425</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #0000ff; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">)</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">unitIdComponents.json</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, now the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">_values</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> keys are arrays instead of space-separated strings (</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16373" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16373</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">)</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">languages.json</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> and other files no longer include some code-fallback data, such as </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">&quot;apc&quot;: &quot;apc&quot;</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> where the translation is the same as the code. </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> (</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16468" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16468</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">)</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> For time zone names, clients will need to construct the fallback exemplar city </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-dates.html#Time_Zone_Names" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">per spec</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">. For example, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">America/Los_Angeles</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> → &quot;Los Angeles&quot; (last field of the TZID, and turn </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">_</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> into space).</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">For language names, see the </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-general.html#locale_display_name_algorithm" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">locale display name algorithm</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">. The &quot;composed&quot; forms are no longer automatically included in the data. For example, purely composed forms such as </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">&quot;en_GB&quot;: &quot;en (GB)&quot;</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> or </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">&quot;en_GB&quot;: &quot;English (United Kingdom)&quot;</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> are no longer present in the JSON data, unless there is an explicit translation such as </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">&quot;en_GB&quot;:&quot;British English&quot;</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Implementations should be aware that some </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">und.json</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> files may now be completely missing due to this change.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">See the Migration section for general data changes.</span></p><div id="h.sz0n2es3i9dl" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.sz0n2es3i9dl_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.sz0n2es3i9dl_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.sz0n2es3i9dl" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.sz0n2es3i9dl_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Specification Changes</span></div></h2><br><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 0.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Please see </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35.html#Modifications" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Modifications</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;"> section in the LDML for full list of items:</span></p><br><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 0.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Removed numbering from sections, to allow for more flexible reorganization of the specification in the future.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 3.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35-personNames.html#Contents" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Person Names</span></a></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 3.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Brought Person Name Formatting out of tech preview.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Described the changes from the fields </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328; font-style: italic;">prefix</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;"> and </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328; font-style: italic;">suffix</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;"> to the fields </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328; font-style: italic;">title</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328; font-style: italic;">generation</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">, and </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328; font-style: italic;">credentials</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">. The problem was that ‘prefix’ and ‘suffix’ are positional terms, whereas the contents may need to change position based on the locale.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Provided much more detailed algorithms for the whole </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35-personNames.html#formatting-process" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Formatting Process</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">, including additional processing steps such as </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35-personNames.html#handle-missing-surname" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Handle missing surname</span></a><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="">.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Documented changes in the </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35-personNames.html#sample-name" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Sample Name</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;"> structure (whose primary use is internal to CLDR data collection).</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">For more background, the </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1mjxIHsb97Og8ub6BKWxOihcHz7zjU4GdFkIxWHGAtes/edit#heading=h.4u6bqbd313a5" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Person Names Guide</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;"> may be helpful, although it is primarily targeted at CLDR data submitters.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 3.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Locales</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Fixed formatting errors in </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35.html#likely-subtags" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; keyword</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328; text-decoration: line-through;">s</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;"> updates in </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-68/tr35.html#Key_And_Type_Definitions_" target="_blank" style="color: inherit;
