border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 3.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1f2328;">Added pointer to the recommended open-source library </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://github.com/google/libphonenumber#what-is-it" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">libphonenumber</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><div id="h.3ne7bix5xy2m" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.3ne7bix5xy2m_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.3ne7bix5xy2m_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.3ne7bix5xy2m" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.3ne7bix5xy2m_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Growth</span></div></h2><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.92; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-top: 11.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">The following chart shows the growth of CLDR locale-specific data over time. It is restricted to data items in</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline;"> /main </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">and</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline;"> /annotations</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> directories, so it does not include the non-locale-specific data. The % values are percent of the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-style: italic; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">current</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> measure of Modern coverage. That level is </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; vertical-align: baseline;">increases</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> each release, so previous releases had many locales that were at Modern coverage as assessed at the time of their release. There is one line per year, even though there were multiple releases in most years.</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.92; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-top: 11.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">The detailed information on changes between v43 release and v42 are at</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://github.com/unicode-org/cldr-staging/blob/main/docs/charts/42/tsv/delta_summary.tsv" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">v43 </span></a><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/cldr/charts/43/tsv/delta_summary.tsv" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">delta_summary.tsv</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; font-variant: normal; vertical-align: baseline;">: look at the TOTAL line for the overall counts of Added/Deleted/Changed.</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.92; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-top: 11.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #212121; font-size: 12.0pt; vertical-align: baseline;">Because this was a limited-submission release, there are a small number of changes visible.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section><section id="h.36635767e929bd4_3" class="yaqOZd"><div purZT-AhqUyc-II5mzb ZcASvf-AhqUyc-II5mzb pSzOP-AhqUyc-qWD73c Ktthjf-AhqUyc-qWD73c JNdkSc SQVYQc"><div class="JNdkSc-SmKAyb LkDMRd"><div class="" jscontroller="sGwD4d" jsaction="zXBUYb:zTPCnb;zQF9Uc:Qxe3nd;" jsname="F57UId"><div class="oKdM2c ZZyype Kzv0Me"><div id="h.36635767e929bd4_0" class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-OiUrBf Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-OiUrBf jXK9ad D2fZ2 zu5uec OjCsFc dmUFtb wHaque g5GTcb"><div class="jXK9ad-SmKAyb"><div class="tyJCtd OWlOyc baZpAe"><div jscontroller="VYKRW" jsaction="rcuQ6b:rcuQ6b;"><div class="WIdY2d M1aSXe"><div jsname="WXxXjd" 6.41V10h2V3h-7z"/></svg></a><iframe jsname="L5Fo6c" class="YMEQtf KfXz0b" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-popups allow-forms allow-same-origin allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-downloads allow-modals LkDMRd"><div class="" jscontroller="sGwD4d" jsaction="zXBUYb:zTPCnb;zQF9Uc:Qxe3nd;" jsname="F57UId"></div></div></div></div></div></section><section id="h.7dc9c2572f0b9895_36" class="yaqOZd"><div class="IFuOkc"></div><div class="mYVXT"><div class="LS81yb VICjCf j5pSsc db35Fc" tabindex="-1"><div class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd purZT-AhqUyc-II5mzb ZcASvf-AhqUyc-II5mzb pSzOP-AhqUyc-qWD73c Ktthjf-AhqUyc-qWD73c JNdkSc SQVYQc"><div class="JNdkSc-SmKAyb LkDMRd"><div class="" jscontroller="sGwD4d" jsaction="zXBUYb:zTPCnb;zQF9Uc:Qxe3nd;" jsname="F57UId"><div class="oKdM2c ZZyype Kzv0Me"><div id="h.7dc9c2572f0b9895_39" class="hJDwNd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd Ft7HRd-AhqUyc-uQSCkd jXK9ad D2fZ2 zu5uec OjCsFc dmUFtb wHaque g5GTcb"><div class="jXK9ad-SmKAyb"><div class="tyJCtd mGzaTb Depvyb baZpAe"><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 3.0pt; margin-top: 0.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="KB0Tx C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline;">Language Matching</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">CLDR has data for </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-style: italic;">language matching</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, as in</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode.org/cldr/charts/43/supplemental/language_matching.html" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #1155cc; text-decoration: underline;">this chart</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">. The purpose and usage is sometimes misunderstood. </span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">So how is this used? Consider a user whose first language is Breton. If they open an application that only has localizations for English, German, and French, then Breton will not be available. In that case, the data in CLDR can be used to select French as a fallback localization — </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-style: italic;">in the absence of other information.</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> </span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">That last clause is important. The CLDR data is based on the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-style: italic;">likelihood</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> that a person using language X understands text written in language Y, but large portions of the population for X might prefer other languages. </span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The CLDR language matching data can </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-style: italic;">and should</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> be overridden whenever there is more information available from a user that allows an implementation to do a better job. It is </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-style: italic; font-weight: 700;">strongly recommended</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> that systems allow users to not only specify their preferred language, but also any secondary languages in order of priority. Thus a person speaking Kazakh who also knows French could specify French as a secondary language, and get a French localization for an app instead of the CLDR match. This has been done on both Android and iOS, for example.</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-left: 36.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Important:  </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">language matching is different from the CLDR </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-style: italic;">inheritance mechanism:</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> they serve different purposes, and are not aligned. The CLDR inheritance mechanism is how CLDR organizes localized data, and </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-style: italic;">should not</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> be used for language matching. Applications do not need to follow the CLDR inheritance chain.</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.44; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-left: 36.0pt; margin-top: 6.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">References: </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/#LanguageMatching" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">LDML Language Matching</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/#Inheritance_vs_Related" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">LDML Inheritance vs Related Information</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">,</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.github.io/icu-docs/apidoc/released/icu4j/index.html?com/ibm/icu/util/LocaleMatcher.html" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">ICU4J Locale Matcher</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="">, </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.github.io/icu-docs/apidoc/released/icu4c/localematcher_8h.html#details" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">ICU4C Locale Matcher</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> </span></p><div id="h.7s25aqdv767e" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.7s25aqdv767e_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div role="presentation" class="U26fgb mUbCce fKz7Od LRAOtb Znu9nd M9Bg4d" jscontroller="mxS5xe" jsaction="click:cOuCgd; mousedown:UX7yZ; mouseup:lbsD7e; mouseenter:tfO1Yc; mouseleave:JywGue; focus:AHmuwe; blur:O22p3e; contextmenu:mg9Pef;" jsshadow aria-describedby="h.7s25aqdv767e_l" aria-label="Copy heading link" aria-disabled="false" data-tooltip="Copy heading link" aria-hidden="true" data-tooltip-position="top" data-tooltip-vertical-offset="12" data-tooltip-horizontal-offset="0"><a class="FKF6mc TpQm9d" href="cldr-43#h.7s25aqdv767e" aria-label="Copy heading link" jsname="hiK3ld" role="button" aria-describedby="h.7s25aqdv767e_l"><div class="VTBa7b MbhUzd" jsname="ksKsZd"></div><span jsslot class="xjKiLb"><span class="Ce1Y1c" style="top: -11px"><svg class="OUGEr QdAdhf" width="22px" height="22px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"/></svg></span></span></a></div></div><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Migration</span></div></h2><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Seed has been merged into Common (</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-6396" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-6396</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">)</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">All files have been moved from the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">seed/</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> to the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">common/</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> subdirectory.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Implementations should make use of the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">common/properties/coverageLevels.txt</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> file</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> (added in CLDR v41) to filter locale files appropriately, in place of depending on incomplete files being in seed. This file and its usage is documented at </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://cldr.unicode.org/index/cldr-spec/coverage-levels" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">Coverage Levels</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">. (</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16420" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16420</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">).</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="">Background: </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Older versions of CLDR separated some locale files into a &#39;seed&#39; directory, which some implementations used for filtering, but the criteria for moving from seed to common were not rigorous. To maintain compatibility with </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="">its</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> set of locales used from previous versions, an implementation may use the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">coverageLevels.txt</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> file</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> filtering</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> for Basic and above, but then also add locales that were previously included.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Interval Formats</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">A small number of interval formats (like “Dec 2 – 3”) have their spacing changed for consistency. This is unlikely to cause problems, as they are similar to a large number of similar changes in v42.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Person Name Formatting</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">Person Name Formatting </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">was in</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> Tech Preview, to allow for</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;"> feedback. It has now advanced out of Tech Preview </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">and can be used in production. We will continue to enhance the data in subsequent releases</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">, but will now maintain compatibility.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">The field structure for the p</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">erson name patterns was changed while in Tech Preview. This </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">changed </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">two</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> field values (</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">prefix</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">suffix</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">) to be more </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">semantically based</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> (</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">title</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">generation</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">credentials</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">) instead of positionally </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">based</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">, splitting the suffix because the placement may vary.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The handling of literals between placeholders in patterns has also changed. For example, when the pattern “</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 400;">{given}•{given2}•{surname}</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">” is used to format a name record [given=Albert, surname=Einstein], the missing field is collapsed and the adjacent literals coalesced, given the equivalent of the pattern </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">“</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400;">{given}•{surname}</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">”, and thus yielding “Albert•Einstein” rather than “Albert••Einstein”. Bef</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">orehand, translators would have to supply an extra pattern to avoid the •• result.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The handling of spaces in the final formatted string has also changed.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">The specification has been substantially revised to more clearly provide the exact steps to take in formatting a name, so any code formatting person names using the tech preview from v42 must be carefully reviewed and adjusted as necessary.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Collation</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">As usual when there are collation changes, databases may need to re-index sorted fields.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Locale Inheritance</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">The parentLocales now have an optional </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #188038; font-variant: normal;">component</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> attribute. This attribute </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">MUST</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> not simply be ignored; otherwise data from different components </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">could</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> override the main parentLocale data. The attribute specifies inheritance adjustments that should be used for </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-style: italic; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">segmentations</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> or </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-style: italic; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">collations</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">. For example, zh_Hant does not normally inherit from zh (since people would </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">get </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">mixed scripts). However, collations can be designed to handle sets of characters for multiple writing systems.</span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0.0pt; margin-left: 0.0pt; margin-top: 0.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">Items marked as rgScope should have different inheritance lookup, which is recommended for the best results. However, implementations that use the general inheritance lookup will see no changes.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">Other New Attributes</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">Calendar metadata now has new era attributes (</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">code</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> &amp; </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">aliases</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">), and element </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">inheritEras, </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">all of which may be ignored if not supported.  (</span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode-org.atlassian.net/browse/CLDR-16469" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">CLDR-16469</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">) </span></p></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">Likely Subtags now have an attribute to indicate the </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700;">origin</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;"> of the data. This is informational, and typically be ignored by implementations.</span></p></li></ul></li><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, Arial; font-weight: 700;">Turkey / Türkiye</span></p><ul class="n8H08c UVNKR " style="list-style-type: square; margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0; padding: 0;"><li  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q TYR86d eD0Rn " style="margin-left: 15.0pt;"><p  dir="ltr" role="presentation" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="line-height: 1.38; margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">In v42, the customary English name for the country code TR was &quot;Turkey&quot;, and an alternate name was &quot;</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">Türkiye&quot;. In v43, the customary En</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">glish name was changed to </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">&quot;Türkiye&quot;, and </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">the alternate name was set to </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000; font-variant: normal;">&quot;Turkey&quot;. Translators were advised of </span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">the change, and reviewed the names in their locales to see if any needed adjustment. Implementations that wish to retain the English name &quot;Turkey&quot; may choose to use the alternate form.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><div id="h.8cl3th3e7os2" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.8cl3th3e7os2_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; normal;">Known Issues</span></div></h2><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="margin-left: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; text-indent: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #000000;">None currently.</span></p><div id="h.ypaf2c1741je" class="CobnVe yMxPgf  aP9Z7e"></div><h2 id="h.ypaf2c1741je_l" dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q JYVBee CDt4Ke " style=""><div jscontroller="Ae65rd" jsaction="touchstart:UrsOsc; click:KjsqPd; focusout:QZoaZ; mouseover:y0pDld; mouseout:dq0hvd;fv1Rjc:jbFSOd;CrfLRd:SzACGe;" class="CjVfdc"><div class="PPhIP rviiZ" jsname="haAclf"><div class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Acknowledgments</span></div></h2><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">Many people have made text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">Terms of Use</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;"> apply to CLDR data; in particular, see </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://unicode.org/copyright.html#Exhibit1" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline;">Exhibit 1</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">.</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style=""><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant: normal;">For web pages with different views of CLDR data, see </span><a class="XqQF9c" href="https://cldr.unicode.org/index/charts" target="_blank" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;"><span class="C9DxTc aw5Odc " style="text-decoration: underline;">https://cldr.unicode.org/index/charts</span></a><span class="C9DxTc " style="font-variant:
